- [M7 Cologne](https://www.glam-moda.com/products/m7-cologne-by-yves-saint-laurent): Eau De Toilette Spray M7 by Yves Saint Laurent represents a groundbreaking moment in the realm of luxury fragrances. Released in 2002, this signature scent marks the first in collaboration with renowned designer Tom Ford during his tenure at YSL. Recognized for its pioneering approach, M7 Cologne was one of the earliest fragrances to embrace the boldness of oud—a warm, complex, and richly resinous note. It embodies the iconic fusion of East and West, elegantly merging modern sensibilities with timeless traditions. M7 has stood the test of time as a fragrant embodiment of audacity and charisma, creating an unmistakable imprint in the world of men's perfumes. Fragrance Family: Woody Oriental Scent Type: Rich, Bold, Spicy Notes: The M7 Cologne unravels with a vibrant crescendo of top notes featuring mandarin, bergamot, and a subtle whisper of rosemary—a refreshing yet intriguing prelude. As the fragrance blossoms, the heart reveals an opulent synergy of oud wood and vetiver. The oud here is both raw and refined, offering a smoky, seductive quality perfectly balanced with the earthy green of vetiver. The base features a luxurious blend of musk, amber, and myrrh, providing a deep, warm trail that lingers with a profound sense of mystery and allure. This sophisticated composition highlights the transformative power of each element, capturing an intoxicating essence that captivates the senses. Suggested Use For optimal effect and enduring wear of M7 Cologne, apply the fragrance strategically to pulse points—such as the wrists, neck, and behind the ears. The warmth emanating from these areas intensifies the fragrance, ensuring a fuller development throughout the day. For an enhanced experience, consider applying it on warmer skin, just after showering, allowing the enchanting notes to amplify and resonate deeply, revealing the full spectrum of its complexity. This fragrance has moderate sillage and moderate longevity, making it a versatile fragrance that can be used for any event.Acqua Di Parma is company that began as a small factory in Parma in 1916. It created its first fragrance, Colonia, which was originally used on gentleman’s handkerchiefs to add an enjoyable scent. The company initially did well but eventually hit a slow period. In 1993, three Italians decided to revive the brand. The first boutique was opened in 1998. The company has since become a lifestyle and fashion company, producing fragrances along with candles, bathrobes, and leather accessories. This brilliant blend of notes results in a unique and magical smell that is both fresh and energizing.
